NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

1112

TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE

[Part VI—Sec. 4

In the Matter of Companies Act, 1956
IN THE MATTER OF NATCOM FOODS LIMITED
At an Extraordinary General Meeting of the Company held on 29th April, 2013 at the Registered Office at Plot No. 1740,
1st Floor, I-Block, 5th Street, Anna Nagar West, Chennai-600 040, the following resolution was passed to voluntarily wind
up Natcom Foods Limited.
RESOLVED THAT having regard to the declaration of solvency dated 30th March, 2013, made by the Board of
Directors of the Company under Section 488 of the Companies Act, 1956, stating that the Company would be able to pay
its debts in full within a period of three years from the date of declaration thereof, the Company, having its Registered Office
at Plot No. 1740, 1st Floor, I-Block, 5th Street, Anna Nagar West, Chennai-600 040, be wound up voluntarily, pursuant to
Section 484 (1) (b) of the Companies Act, 1956.
Chennai,
3-5-2013.

K. RAVICHANDRAN,
Director.

PRINTED AND PUBLISHED BY THE DIRECTOR OF STATIONERY AND PRINTING, CHENNAI
ON BEHALF OF THE GOVERNMENT OF TAMIL NADU
